The user interface is designed to make it easy to work on all these devices. For example: keyboard shortcuts on PC/tablet with physical keyboard; on-screen context menu to perform typical editing actions like Cut/Copy/Paste and text selection.\r\n\r\nThis app registers .tex file extension so you can pick it as default app to open your LaTeX documents.\r\n\r\nThe sample LawTeX introduction beamer slide (in the screenshot) can be obtained at https://1drv.ms/u/s!AhSl9YDS4Yt4hBOPO7DDGrqI0Vkd \r\n\r\nIMPORTANT\r\n\r\n * For long, we ABANDONED Windows 8.1 and Windows Phone 8.1 versions.
